## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of concentration dA/dt in a chemical reaction, where the rate typically depends on the current concentration A through rate laws of various orders, and possibly on time t for non-autonomous or externally driven reactions.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction of same species)
- nth-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate law)
- Mixed first-order with constant source: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (first-order with production/inflow)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (approach to equilibrium A тЗМ B)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme-catalyzed or saturation kinetics)
- Autocatalytic: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (logistic-type autocatalysis A + B тЖТ 2A)
- Second-order with equilibrium: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 + c1 * A + c2 (reversible bimolecular reaction)
- Inhibition kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A**2) (substrate inhibition)
- Time-dependent forcing: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * t (time-varying external influence)
- Exponential time modulation: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (temperature ramp via Arrhenius)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (Hill-type cooperative binding)
- Parallel reactions: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (competing first and second order pathways)
- Fractional order with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (fractional order with background rate)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope тЖТ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects тЖТ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay тЖТ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior тЖТ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects тЖТ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Concentration power-law dependence тЖТ reaction order: dA_dt тИЭ A**n indicates an nth-order elementary or apparent reaction
- Product of concentration and (constant - concentration) тЖТ autocatalytic or logistic kinetics where both reactant and product participate
- Rational function of concentration (A/(K+A)) тЖТ saturation kinetics typical of enzyme-catalyzed or surface-catalyzed reactions
- Sum of multiple power-law terms in A тЖТ parallel competing reaction pathways with different orders
- Negative coefficient on A terms тЖТ consumption/decay of reactant; positive coefficient тЖТ production or autocatalysis
- Explicit time dependence combined with concentration тЖТ non-isothermal conditions or time-varying external stimulus (e.g., light intensity)
- Quadratic polynomial in A тЖТ reversible bimolecular reaction kinetics near equilibrium or two competing pathways
- Rate approaching zero as AтЖТ0 with nonlinear curvature тЖТ fractional or Michaelis-Menten type kinetics rather than simple integer order
